      401            01  FILLER                    PIC  X(050) VALUE
      402                '*** FIM DA WORKING-STORAGE ***'.
      403
      404           ******************************************************************
      405            PROCEDURE DIVISION.
      406           ******************************************************************

DB2 SQL PRECOMPILER         VERSION 12 REL. 1.0                                                       PAGE 9
      407
      408           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      409            0000-ROTINA-PRINCIPAL           SECTION.
      410           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      411
      412                PERFORM 1000-INICIO
      413
      414                PERFORM 5000-PROCESSO
      415                  UNTIL WRK-FS-EAQALPHA    EQUAL '10'
      416                    AND WRK-FS-EAQMATRZ    EQUAL '10'
      417
      418                PERFORM 9000-FINALIZA
      419
      420                GOBACK
      421                .
      422           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      423            0000-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      424           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      425
      426           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      427            1000-INICIO                     SECTION.
      428           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      429
      430                CALL 'CKRS1000'
      431
      432                PERFORM 8000-INICIO-CKRS0100
      433
      434                OPEN INPUT EAQALPHA
      435                           EAQMATRZ
      436
      437                MOVE WRK-ABERTURA           TO WRK-OPERACAO
      438
      439                PERFORM 1100-TESTAR-FS-EAQALPHA
      440
      441                PERFORM 1110-TESTAR-FS-EAQMATRZ
      442
      443                PERFORM 1200-LER-EAQMATRZ
      444
      445                PERFORM 1220-LER-EAQALPHA
      446                .
      447           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      448            1000-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      449           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      450
      451           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      452            1100-TESTAR-FS-EAQALPHA         SECTION.
      453           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      454
      455                IF WRK-FS-EAQALPHA          NOT EQUAL '00' AND '10'
      456                    MOVE 'APL'              TO ERR-TIPO-ACESSO
      457                    MOVE 'EAQALPHA'         TO WRK-NOME-ARQ
      458                    MOVE WRK-FS-EAQALPHA    TO WRK-FILE-STATUS
      459                    MOVE WRK-MSG-FS-ERRO    TO ERR-TEXTO
      460                    PERFORM 9999-ROTINA-ERRO
      461                END-IF
      462                .
      463           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      464            1100-99-FIM.                    EXIT.

DB2 SQL PRECOMPILER         VERSION 12 REL. 1.0                                                       PAGE 10
      465           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      466
      467           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      468            1110-TESTAR-FS-EAQMATRZ         SECTION.
      469           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      470
      471                IF WRK-FS-EAQMATRZ          NOT EQUAL '00' AND '10'
      472                   MOVE 'APL'               TO ERR-TIPO-ACESSO
      473                   MOVE 'EAQMATRZ'          TO WRK-NOME-ARQ
      474                   MOVE WRK-FS-EAQMATRZ     TO WRK-FILE-STATUS
      475                   MOVE WRK-MSG-FS-ERRO     TO ERR-TEXTO
      476                   PERFORM 9999-ROTINA-ERRO
      477                END-IF
      478                .
      479           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      480            1110-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      481           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      482
      483           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      484            1200-LER-EAQMATRZ               SECTION.
      485           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      486
      487                READ EAQMATRZ
      488
      489                MOVE WRK-LEITURA            TO WRK-OPERACAO
      490
      491                PERFORM 1110-TESTAR-FS-EAQMATRZ
      492
      493                IF WRK-FS-EAQMATRZ          EQUAL '00'
      494                   MOVE FD-MTZ-CSGMTO-EMPR       TO WRK-MTZ-CSGMTO-EMPR
      495                   MOVE FD-MTZ-CEMPR-CONVN-ARRE  TO WRK-MTZ-CEMPR-CONVN-ARRE
      496                   MOVE FD-MTZ-CTRIBT-ARRE       TO WRK-MTZ-CTRIBT-ARRE
      497                   MOVE FD-MTZ-CVRSAO-COD-BARRA  TO WRK-MTZ-CVRSAO-COD-BARRA
      498
      499                   MOVE FD-MTZ-DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ(1:2) TO WRK-DT-AUX(7:2)
      500                   MOVE FD-MTZ-DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ(4:2) TO WRK-DT-AUX(5:2)
      501                   MOVE FD-MTZ-DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ(7:4) TO WRK-DT-AUX(1:4)
      502                   MOVE WRK-DT-AUX-N             TO WRK-MTZ-DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ
      503
      504                   MOVE FD-MTZ-CCPO-PARM-BARRA   TO WRK-MTZ-CCPO-PARM-BARRA
      505                   MOVE FD-MTZ-CSEQ-PARM-ARRE    TO WRK-MTZ-CSEQ-PARM-ARRE
      506                   ADD 1                         TO WRK-ACU-LIDOS-EAQMATRZ
      507                ELSE
      508                    MOVE HIGH-VALUES        TO FD-CHAVE-MATRIZ
      509                END-IF
      510                .
      511           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      512            1200-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      513           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      514
      515           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      516            1220-LER-EAQALPHA               SECTION.
      517           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      518
      519                READ EAQALPHA
      520
      521                MOVE WRK-LEITURA            TO  WRK-OPERACAO
      522

DB2 SQL PRECOMPILER         VERSION 12 REL. 1.0                                                       PAGE 11
      523                PERFORM 1100-TESTAR-FS-EAQALPHA
      524
      525                IF WRK-FS-EAQALPHA          EQUAL '00'
      526                   ADD 1                    TO WRK-ACU-LIDOS-EAQALPHA
      527                   MOVE FD-ALP-CSGMTO-EMPR       TO WRK-ALP-CSGMTO-EMPR
      528                   MOVE FD-ALP-CEMPR-CONVN-ARRE  TO WRK-ALP-CEMPR-CONVN-ARRE
      529                   MOVE FD-ALP-CTRIBT-ARRE       TO WRK-ALP-CTRIBT-ARRE
      530                   MOVE FD-ALP-CVRSAO-COD-BARRA  TO WRK-ALP-CVRSAO-COD-BARRA
      531
      532                   MOVE FD-ALP-DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ(1:2) TO WRK-DT-AUX(7:2)
      533                   MOVE FD-ALP-DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ(4:2) TO WRK-DT-AUX(5:2)
      534                   MOVE FD-ALP-DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ(7:4) TO WRK-DT-AUX(1:4)
      535                   MOVE WRK-DT-AUX-N             TO WRK-ALP-DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ
      536
      537                   MOVE FD-ALP-CCPO-PARM-BARRA   TO WRK-ALP-CCPO-PARM-BARRA
      538                   MOVE FD-ALP-CSEQ-PARM-ARRE    TO WRK-ALP-CSEQ-PARM-ARRE
      539                ELSE
      540                   MOVE HIGH-VALUES              TO FD-CHAVE-ALPHA
      541                END-IF
      542                .
      543           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      544            1220-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      545           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      546
      547           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      548            5000-PROCESSO                   SECTION.
      549           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      550
      551
      552                IF WRK-CHAVE-MTZ            EQUAL WRK-CHAVE-ALP
      553                   IF WRK-REG-MTZ           NOT EQUAL WRK-REG-ALP
      554                      PERFORM 5200-UPDATE-CBARB006
      555                   END-IF
      556
      557                   PERFORM 1200-LER-EAQMATRZ
      558
      559                   PERFORM 1220-LER-EAQALPHA
      560                ELSE
      561                    IF WRK-CHAVE-MTZ      GREATER WRK-CHAVE-ALP
      562                       PERFORM 5100-INSERT-CBARB006
      563
      564                       PERFORM 1220-LER-EAQALPHA
      565                    ELSE
      566                       ADD 1                TO ACU-MATRIZ-SEM-ALPHA
      567
      568                       PERFORM 1200-LER-EAQMATRZ
      569                    END-IF
      570                END-IF
      571                .
      572           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      573            5000-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      574           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      575
      576           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      577            5100-INSERT-CBARB006            SECTION.
      578           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      579
      580                INITIALIZE                  CBARB006

DB2 SQL PRECOMPILER         VERSION 12 REL. 1.0                                                       PAGE 12
      581                                            WRK-NULIDADE
      582                                            REPLACING ALPHANUMERIC BY SPACES
      583                                            NUMERIC BY ZEROS
      584
      585                PERFORM 5300-MOVIMENTACAO
      586
      587                PERFORM 5350-NULIDADE
      588
      589                EXEC SQL
      590                  INSERT INTO DB2PRD.CAMPO_BARRA
      591                        (CSGMTO_EMPR
      592                        ,CEMPR_CONVN_ARRE
      593                        ,CTRIBT_ARRE
      594                        ,CVRSAO_COD_BARRA
      595                        ,DVALDD_INIC_PARMZ
      596                        ,CCPO_PARM_BARRA
      597                        ,CSEQ_PARM_ARRE
      598                        ,MTMNHO_PARM_BARRA
      599                        ,CPOSIC_PARM_BARRA
      600                        ,RDMNIO_COD_BARRA
      601                        ,RFAIXA_INIC_BARRA
      602                        ,RFAIXA_FNAL_BARRA
      603                        ,CPOSIC_INIC_DIG
      604                        ,CPOSIC_FNAL_DIG
      605                        ,CMDULO_DIG_VERIF
      606                        ,CPOSIC_INIC_SAIDA)
      607                  VALUES
      608                        (:CBARB006.CSGMTO-EMPR
      609                        ,:CBARB006.CEMPR-CONVN-ARRE
      610                        ,:CBARB006.CTRIBT-ARRE
      611                        ,:CBARB006.CVRSAO-COD-BARRA
      612                        ,:CBARB006.DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ
      613                        ,:CBARB006.CCPO-PARM-BARRA
      614                        ,:CBARB006.CSEQ-PARM-ARRE
      615                        ,:CBARB006.MTMNHO-PARM-BARRA
      616                        ,:CBARB006.CPOSIC-PARM-BARRA
      617                        ,:CBARB006.RDMNIO-COD-BARRA
      618                              :WRK-RDMNIO-COD-BARRA-N
      619                        ,:CBARB006.RFAIXA-INIC-BARRA
      620                              :WRK-RFAIXA-INIC-BARRA-N
      621                        ,:CBARB006.RFAIXA-FNAL-BARRA
      622                              :WRK-RFAIXA-FNAL-BARRA-N
      623                        ,:CBARB006.CPOSIC-INIC-DIG
      624                              :WRK-CPOSIC-INIC-DIG-N
      625                        ,:CBARB006.CPOSIC-FNAL-DIG
      626                              :WRK-CPOSIC-FNAL-DIG-N
      627                        ,:CBARB006.CMDULO-DIG-VERIF
      628                              :WRK-CMDULO-DIG-VERIF-N
      629                        ,:CBARB006.CPOSIC-INIC-SAIDA)
      630                END-EXEC
      631
      632                IF SQLCODE                  NOT EQUAL ZEROS
      633                OR SQLWARN0                 EQUAL 'W'
      634                   MOVE 'DB2'               TO ERR-TIPO-ACESSO
      635                   MOVE 'CBARX266'          TO ERR-PGM
      636                   MOVE 'CAMPO_BARRA'       TO ERR-DBD-TAB
      637                   MOVE 'INSERT'            TO ERR-FUN-COMANDO
      638                   MOVE SQLCODE             TO ERR-SQL-CODE

DB2 SQL PRECOMPILER         VERSION 12 REL. 1.0                                                       PAGE 13
      639                   MOVE '0008'              TO ERR-LOCAL
      640                   MOVE SPACES              TO ERR-SEGM
      641                   PERFORM  9999-ROTINA-ERRO
      642                END-IF
      643
      644                ADD 1                       TO ACU-INSERT-CBARB006
      645
      646                PERFORM 8100-CHECKPOINT-CKRS0100
      647                .
      648           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      649            5100-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      650           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      651
      652           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      653            5200-UPDATE-CBARB006            SECTION.
      654           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      655
      656                INITIALIZE                  CBARB006
      657                                            WRK-NULIDADE
      658                                            REPLACING ALPHANUMERIC BY SPACES
      659                                            NUMERIC BY ZEROS
      660
      661                PERFORM 5300-MOVIMENTACAO
      662
      663                PERFORM 5350-NULIDADE
      664
      665                EXEC SQL
      666                  UPDATE DB2PRD.CAMPO_BARRA
      667                     SET MTMNHO_PARM_BARRA  = :CBARB006.MTMNHO-PARM-BARRA
      668                        ,CPOSIC_PARM_BARRA  = :CBARB006.CPOSIC-PARM-BARRA
      669                        ,RDMNIO_COD_BARRA   = :CBARB006.RDMNIO-COD-BARRA
      670                         :WRK-RDMNIO-COD-BARRA-N
      671                        ,RFAIXA_INIC_BARRA  = :CBARB006.RFAIXA-INIC-BARRA
      672                         :WRK-RFAIXA-INIC-BARRA-N
      673                        ,RFAIXA_FNAL_BARRA  = :CBARB006.RFAIXA-FNAL-BARRA
      674                         :WRK-RFAIXA-FNAL-BARRA-N
      675                        ,CPOSIC_INIC_DIG    = :CBARB006.CPOSIC-INIC-DIG
      676                         :WRK-CPOSIC-INIC-DIG-N
      677                        ,CPOSIC_FNAL_DIG    = :CBARB006.CPOSIC-FNAL-DIG
      678                         :WRK-CPOSIC-FNAL-DIG-N
      679                        ,CMDULO_DIG_VERIF   = :CBARB006.CMDULO-DIG-VERIF
      680                         :WRK-CMDULO-DIG-VERIF-N
      681                        ,CPOSIC_INIC_SAIDA  = :CBARB006.CPOSIC-INIC-SAIDA
      682                   WHERE CSGMTO_EMPR        = :CBARB006.CSGMTO-EMPR
      683                     AND CEMPR_CONVN_ARRE   = :CBARB006.CEMPR-CONVN-ARRE
      684                     AND CTRIBT_ARRE        = :CBARB006.CTRIBT-ARRE
      685                     AND CVRSAO_COD_BARRA   = :CBARB006.CVRSAO-COD-BARRA
      686                     AND DVALDD_INIC_PARMZ  = :CBARB006.DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ
      687                     AND CCPO_PARM_BARRA    = :CBARB006.CCPO-PARM-BARRA
      688                     AND CSEQ_PARM_ARRE     = :CBARB006.CSEQ-PARM-ARRE
      689                END-EXEC
      690
      691                IF SQLCODE                  NOT EQUAL ZEROS
      692                OR SQLWARN0                 EQUAL 'W'
      693                   MOVE 'DB2'               TO ERR-TIPO-ACESSO
      694                   MOVE 'CBARX266'          TO ERR-PGM
      695                   MOVE 'CAMPO_BARRA'       TO ERR-DBD-TAB
      696                   MOVE 'UPDATE'            TO ERR-FUN-COMANDO

DB2 SQL PRECOMPILER         VERSION 12 REL. 1.0                                                       PAGE 14
      697                   MOVE SQLCODE             TO ERR-SQL-CODE
      698                   MOVE '0009'              TO ERR-LOCAL
      699                   MOVE SPACES              TO ERR-SEGM
      700                   PERFORM  9999-ROTINA-ERRO
      701                END-IF
      702
      703                ADD 1                       TO ACU-UPDATE-CBARB006
      704
      705                PERFORM 8100-CHECKPOINT-CKRS0100
      706                .
      707           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      708            5200-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      709           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      710
      711           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      712            5300-MOVIMENTACAO               SECTION.
      713           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      714                MOVE FD-ALP-CSGMTO-EMPR      TO CSGMTO-EMPR       OF CBARB006
      715                MOVE FD-ALP-CEMPR-CONVN-ARRE
      716                                             TO CEMPR-CONVN-ARRE  OF CBARB006
      717                MOVE FD-ALP-CTRIBT-ARRE      TO CTRIBT-ARRE       OF CBARB006
      718                MOVE FD-ALP-CVRSAO-COD-BARRA TO CVRSAO-COD-BARRA  OF CBARB006
      719                MOVE FD-ALP-DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ
      720                                             TO DVALDD-INIC-PARMZ OF CBARB006
      721                MOVE FD-ALP-CCPO-PARM-BARRA  TO CCPO-PARM-BARRA   OF CBARB006
      722                MOVE FD-ALP-CSEQ-PARM-ARRE   TO CSEQ-PARM-ARRE    OF CBARB006
      723                MOVE FD-ALP-MTMNHO-PARM-BARRA
      724                                             TO MTMNHO-PARM-BARRA OF CBARB006
      725                MOVE FD-ALP-CPOSIC-PARM-BARRA
      726                                             TO CPOSIC-PARM-BARRA OF CBARB006
      727                MOVE FD-ALP-RDMNIO-COD-BARRA TO RDMNIO-COD-BARRA  OF CBARB006
      728                MOVE FD-ALP-RFAIXA-INIC-BARRA
      729                                             TO RFAIXA-INIC-BARRA OF CBARB006
      730                MOVE FD-ALP-RFAIXA-FNAL-BARRA
      731                                             TO RFAIXA-FNAL-BARRA OF CBARB006
      732                MOVE FD-ALP-CPOSIC-INIC-DIG  TO CPOSIC-INIC-DIG   OF CBARB006
      733                MOVE FD-ALP-CPOSIC-FNAL-DIG  TO CPOSIC-FNAL-DIG   OF CBARB006
      734                MOVE FD-ALP-CMDULO-DIG-VERIF TO CMDULO-DIG-VERIF  OF CBARB006
      735                MOVE FD-ALP-CPOSIC-INIC-SAIDA
      736                                             TO CPOSIC-INIC-SAIDA OF CBARB006
      737
      738                .
      739           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      740            5300-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      741           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      742
      743           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      744            5350-NULIDADE                   SECTION.
      745           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      746
      747                IF FD-ALP-RDMNIO-COD-BARRA-N EQUAL '?'
      748                   MOVE -1                  TO WRK-RDMNIO-COD-BARRA-N
      749                   MOVE SPACES              TO RDMNIO-COD-BARRA OF CBARB006
      750                END-IF
      751
      752                IF FD-ALP-RFAIXA-INIC-BARRA-N   EQUAL '?'
      753                   MOVE -1                  TO WRK-RFAIXA-INIC-BARRA-N
      754                   MOVE SPACES              TO RFAIXA-INIC-BARRA OF CBARB006

DB2 SQL PRECOMPILER         VERSION 12 REL. 1.0                                                       PAGE 15
      755                END-IF
      756
      757                IF FD-ALP-RFAIXA-FNAL-BARRA-N   EQUAL '?'
      758                   MOVE -1                  TO WRK-RFAIXA-FNAL-BARRA-N
      759                   MOVE SPACES              TO RFAIXA-FNAL-BARRA OF CBARB006
      760                END-IF
      761
      762                IF FD-ALP-CPOSIC-INIC-DIG-N     EQUAL '?'
      763                   MOVE -1                  TO WRK-CPOSIC-INIC-DIG-N
      764                   MOVE ZEROS               TO CPOSIC-INIC-DIG  OF CBARB006
      765                END-IF
      766
      767                IF FD-ALP-CPOSIC-FNAL-DIG-N     EQUAL '?'
      768                   MOVE -1                  TO WRK-CPOSIC-FNAL-DIG-N
      769                   MOVE ZEROS               TO CPOSIC-FNAL-DIG  OF CBARB006
      770                END-IF
      771
      772                IF FD-ALP-CMDULO-DIG-VERIF-N    EQUAL '?'
      773                   MOVE -1                  TO WRK-CMDULO-DIG-VERIF-N
      774                   MOVE ZEROS               TO CMDULO-DIG-VERIF OF CBARB006
      775                END-IF
      776                .
      777           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      778            5350-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      779           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      780
      781           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      782            8000-INICIO-CKRS0100            SECTION.
      783           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      784
      785                INITIALIZE                  CKRS01-INTERFACE
      786                                            REPLACING ALPHANUMERIC BY SPACES
      787                                            NUMERIC BY ZEROS
      788
      789                MOVE 'DB2 '                 TO  CK01-ID-DB2
      790                MOVE 'I'                    TO  CK01-FUNCAO
      791                MOVE LENGTH OF WRK-AREA-RESTART
      792                                            TO  CK01-TAM-AREA-RESTART
      793
      794                PERFORM 8300-CHAMAR-CKRS0100
      795
      796                IF CK01-STATUS              EQUAL 'REST'
      797                   MOVE CK01-AREA-RESTART(1:CK01-TAM-AREA-RESTART) TO
      798                                                             WRK-AREA-RESTART
      799                   DISPLAY 'CBARX266 - PROCESSAMENTO COM RESTART.'
      800                ELSE
      801                   DISPLAY 'CBARX266 - PROCESSAMENTO NORMAL (SEM RESTART).'
      802                END-IF
      803                .
      804           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      805            8000-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      806           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      807
      808           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      809            8100-CHECKPOINT-CKRS0100        SECTION.
      810           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      811
      812                INITIALIZE                  CKRS01-INTERFACE

DB2 SQL PRECOMPILER         VERSION 12 REL. 1.0                                                       PAGE 16
      813                                            REPLACING ALPHANUMERIC BY SPACES
      814                                            NUMERIC BY ZEROS
      815
      816                MOVE  'P'                   TO CK01-FUNCAO
      817                MOVE  'DB2 '                TO CK01-ID-DB2
      818                MOVE  WRK-AREA-RESTART      TO CK01-AREA-RESTART
      819                MOVE  LENGTH OF WRK-AREA-RESTART
      820                                            TO CK01-TAM-AREA-RESTART
      821
      822                PERFORM 8300-CHAMAR-CKRS0100
      823                .
      824           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      825            8100-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      826           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      827
      828           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      829            8200-FINALIZA-CKRS0100          SECTION.
      830           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      831
      832                INITIALIZE                  CKRS01-INTERFACE
      833                                            REPLACING ALPHANUMERIC BY SPACES
      834                                            NUMERIC BY ZEROS
      835
      836                MOVE 'F'                    TO CK01-FUNCAO
      837                MOVE 'DB2 '                 TO CK01-ID-DB2
      838
      839                PERFORM 8300-CHAMAR-CKRS0100
      840                .
      841           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      842            8200-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      843           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      844
      845           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      846            8300-CHAMAR-CKRS0100            SECTION.
      847           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      848
      849                CALL WRK-CKRS0100           USING CKRS01-INTERFACE
      850
      851                IF CK01-CODIGO-RETORNO      NOT EQUAL  ZEROS
      852                   DISPLAY '************** CBARX266 **************'
      853                   DISPLAY '*          ERRO NA CKRS0100          *'
      854                   DISPLAY '* RETURN-CODE  =  ' CK01-CODIGO-RETORNO
      855                   DISPLAY '* FUNCAO       =  ' CK01-FUNCAO
      856                   DISPLAY '*      PROCESSAMENTO CANCELADO       *'
      857                   DISPLAY '**************************************'
      858                   MOVE  SPACES             TO ERR-SEGM
      859                   MOVE 'ERRO NA CKRS0100'  TO ERR-TEXTO
      860                   MOVE 'APL'               TO ERR-TIPO-ACESSO
      861                   PERFORM 9999-ROTINA-ERRO
      862                END-IF
      863                .
      864           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      865            8300-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      866           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      867
      868           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      869            9000-FINALIZA                   SECTION.
      870           *----------------------------------------------------------------*

      871
      872                DISPLAY '**************** CBARX266 **************'
      873                DISPLAY '*                                      *'
      874                DISPLAY '*         FIM DE PROCESSAMENTO         *'
      875                DISPLAY '*                                      *'
      876                DISPLAY '*                                      *'
      877                DISPLAY '*  TOTAL EAQMATRZ - LIDOS = ' WRK-ACU-LIDOS-EAQMATRZ
      878                                                             '  *'
      879                DISPLAY '*                                      *'
      880                DISPLAY '*  TOTAL EAQALPHA - LIDOS = ' WRK-ACU-LIDOS-EAQALPHA
      881                                                             '  *'
      882                DISPLAY '*                                      *'
      883                DISPLAY '*  TOTAL CBARB006 - INSRT = ' ACU-INSERT-CBARB006
      884                                                             '  *'
      885                DISPLAY '*                                      *'
      886                DISPLAY '*  TOTAL CBARB006 - UPDAT = ' ACU-UPDATE-CBARB006
      887                                                             '  *'
      888                DISPLAY '*                                      *'
      889                DISPLAY '*  SOBRAS NA MATRIZ       = ' ACU-MATRIZ-SEM-ALPHA
      890                                                             '  *'
      891                DISPLAY '*                                      *'
      892                DISPLAY '**************** CBARX266 **************'
      893
      894                CLOSE  EAQALPHA
      895                       EAQMATRZ
      896
      897                MOVE WRK-FECHAMENTO         TO WRK-OPERACAO
      898
      899                PERFORM  1100-TESTAR-FS-EAQALPHA
      900
      901                PERFORM  1110-TESTAR-FS-EAQMATRZ
      902
      903                PERFORM  8200-FINALIZA-CKRS0100
      904                .
      905           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      906            9000-99-FIM.                    EXIT.
      907           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      908
      909           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      910            9999-ROTINA-ERRO                SECTION.
      911           *----------------------------------------------------------------*
      912
      913                MOVE 'CBARX266'             TO ERR-PGM
      914
      915                IF  ERR-TIPO-ACESSO         EQUAL 'DB2'
      916                    CALL 'BRAD7100'         USING WRK-BATCH
      917                                                  ERRO-AREA
      918                                                  SQLCA
      919                ELSE
      920                    CALL 'BRAD7100'         USING WRK-BATCH
      921                                                  ERRO-AREA

Context usage is indicated by the letter preceding a procedure-name reference.
These letters and their meanings are:
    A = ALTER (procedure-name)
    D = GO TO (procedure-name) DEPENDING ON
    E = End of range of (PERFORM) through (procedure-name)
    G = GO TO (procedure-name)
    P = PERFORM (procedure-name)
    T = (ALTER) TO PROCEED TO (procedure-name)
    U = USE FOR DEBUGGING (procedure-name)
